function OU_ApplyChanges(response) {

    for (var i = 0; i < response.length; i++) {

        var value = response[i].Value;

        if (response[i].ParameterType == "boolean")

            value = (value.toLowerCase() == "true");

 try {

         if(response[i].ParameterType == "string[]" || response[i].ParameterType == "integer[]") 

         OU[response[i].ParameterId](response[i].Values);

         else

         OU[response[i].ParameterId](value);

 }catch(e){}

    }

}
